About

Hello, world! This is Karun Dawadi. I am currently pursuing bachelor's degree in computer science at University of Texas at Arlington. I have reached Junior level and have taken multiple courses involving teaching about operating systems, algorithm and data structure, and other various courses. I am very proficient in multiple programming languages like C, C++, Python, and others.

Among all other things I like computers and my whole life I have been in love with computers. I do not mind working in an computer for 24 hours straight. I love computers in short.

I am from Nepal.

You can follow me on following platforms:

LinkeddIn
@karunDawadi
github
